import { z } from 'zod';\n\n// TDD-0031: Crear Pedido\nexport const crearPedidoSchema = z.object({\n  clienteId: z.string().uuid('clienteId debe ser un UUID v├ílido'),\n  repartoId: z.string().uuid('repartoId debe ser un UUID v├ílido').optional(),\n  items: z\n    .array(\n      z.object({\n        itemId: z.string().uuid('itemId debe ser un UUID v├ílido'),\n        cantidad: z.number().int('La cantidad debe ser un n├║mero entero').min(1, 'La cantidad debe ser mayor a 0'),\n      })\n    )\n    .min(1, 'El pedido debe tener al menos un ├¡tem'),\n});\n\n// TDD-0034: Actualizar Estado (m├íquina de estados)\nexport const actualizarEstadoSchema = z.object({\n  estado: z.enum(['EN_RUTA', 'ENTREGADO', 'NO_ENTREGADO'], {\n    errorMap: () => ({ message: 'Estado inv├ílido. Valores permitidos: EN_RUTA, ENTREGADO, NO_ENTREGADO' }),\n  }),\n});\n\n// TDD-0035: Cancelar Pedido (sin body requerido, motivo opcional)\nexport const cancelarPedidoSchema = z.object({\n  motivo: z\n    .enum(['CLIENTE_AUSENTE', 'DIRECCION_INCORRECTA', 'ACCESO_DENEGADO', 'OTRO'])\n    .optional(),\n});\n\n// TDD-0037: Agregar Item a Pedido\nexport const agregarItemSchema = z.object({\n  itemId: z.string().uuid('itemId debe ser un UUID v├ílido'),\n  cantidad: z.number().int('La cantidad debe ser un n├║mero entero').min(1, 'La cantidad debe ser mayor a 0'),\n});\n\n// TDD-0038: Actualizar Cantidad de Item\nexport const actualizarCantidadItemSchema = z.object({\n  cantidad: z.number().int('La cantidad debe ser un n├║mero entero').min(1, 'La cantidad debe ser mayor a 0'),\n});\n\n// TDD-0033: Listar Pedidos - Query Params\nexport const listarPedidosQuerySchema = z.object({\n  clienteId: z.string().uuid('clienteId debe ser un UUID v├ílido').optional(),\n  estado: z\n    .enum(['PENDIENTE', 'EN_RUTA', 'ENTREGADO', 'NO_ENTREGADO', 'CANCELADO'])\n    .optional(),\n  fechaDesde: z.string().datetime({ message: 'fechaDesde debe ser una fecha ISO v├ílida' }).optional(),\n  fechaHasta: z.string().datetime({ message: 'fechaHasta debe ser una fecha ISO v├ílida' }).optional(),\n  repartoId: z.string().uuid('repartoId debe ser un UUID v├ílido').optional(),\n  page: z.coerce.number().int().min(1).default(1),\n  pageSize: z.coerce.number().int().min(1).max(100).default(20),\n});\n\n// Inferred types\nexport type CrearPedidoInput = z.infer<typeof crearPedidoSchema>;\nexport type ActualizarEstadoInput = z.infer<typeof actualizarEstadoSchema>;\nexport type AgregarItemInput = z.infer<typeof agregarItemSchema>;\nexport type ActualizarCantidadItemInput = z.infer<typeof actualizarCantidadItemSchema>;\nexport type ListarPedidosQuery = z.infer<typeof listarPedidosQuerySchema>;\n

import { prisma } from '../../lib/prisma.js';\nimport { ApiError } from '../../utils/api-error.js';\nimport type { EstadoPedido } from '../../../generated/prisma/enums.js';\n\n// ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ Types ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\ninterface PedidoRaw {\n  id: string;\n  orden: number;\n  estado: string;\n  fecha: Date;\n  creadoEn: Date;\n  deletedAt: Date | null;\n  motivoFalla: string | null;\n  cliente: {\n    id: string;\n    nombre: string;\n    apellido: string;\n    telefono: string;\n    calle: string;\n    numero: string;\n    localidad: string;\n    latitud: number;\n    longitud: number;\n    horarioDesde: string;\n    horarioHasta: string;\n  };\n  reparto: {\n    id: string;\n    fecha: Date;\n  } | null;\n  items: Array<{\n    id: string;\n    cantidad: number;\n    precioUnitario: number;\n    item: {\n      id: string;\n      nombre: string;\n      descripcion: string | null;\n      precio: number;\n      unidad: string;\n      activo: boolean;\n    };\n  }>;\n}\n\n// ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ Format helpers ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\nfunction formatPedidoDetalle(pedido: PedidoRaw) {\n  const items = pedido.items.map((pi) => ({\n    id: pi.id,\n    producto: {\n      id: pi.item.id,\n      nombre: pi.item.nombre,\n      descripcion: pi.item.descripcion ?? undefined,\n      precio: pi.item.precio,\n      unidad: pi.item.unidad,\n    },\n    cantidad: pi.cantidad,\n    precioUnitario: pi.precioUnitario,\n  }));\n\n  const total = items.reduce((sum, i) => sum + i.cantidad * i.precioUnitario, 0);\n\n  return {\n    id: pedido.id,\n    orden: pedido.orden,\n    estado: pedido.estado,\n    fecha: pedido.fecha.toISOString(),\n    fechaAlta: pedido.creadoEn.toISOString(),\n    motivoFalla: pedido.motivoFalla ?? undefined,\n    cliente: {\n      id: pedido.cliente.id,\n      nombre: `${pedido.cliente.nombre} ${pedido.cliente.apellido}`,\n      apellido: pedido.cliente.apellido,\n      telefono: pedido.cliente.telefono,\n      domicilio: {\n        calle: pedido.cliente.calle,\n        numero: pedido.cliente.numero,\n        localidad: pedido.cliente.localidad,\n        latitud: pedido.cliente.latitud,\n        longitud: pedido.cliente.longitud,\n      },\n      horarioDesde: pedido.cliente.horarioDesde,\n      horarioHasta: pedido.cliente.horarioHasta,\n    },\n    items,\n    total,\n    reparto: pedido.reparto\n      ? { id: pedido.reparto.id, fecha: pedido.reparto.fecha.toISOString() }\n      : undefined,\n  };\n}\n\nfunction formatPedidoResumen(pedido: PedidoRaw) {\n  const total = pedido.items.reduce(\n    (sum, i) => sum + i.cantidad * i.precioUnitario,\n    0\n  );\n\n  return {\n    id: pedido.id,\n    orden: pedido.orden,\n    estado: pedido.estado,\n    fecha: pedido.fecha.toISOString(),\n    fechaAlta: pedido.creadoEn.toISOString(),\n    cliente: {\n      id: pedido.cliente.id,\n      nombre: `${pedido.cliente.nombre} ${pedido.cliente.apellido}`,\n    },\n    itemsCount: pedido.items.length,\n    total,\n    reparto: pedido.reparto\n      ? { id: pedido.reparto.id, fecha: pedido.reparto.fecha.toISOString() }\n      : undefined,\n  };\n}\n\n// ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ Include helper ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\nconst ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\n/** GET /pedidos/hoy ÔÇö Obtener pedidos del d├¡a para un repartidor */\nexport async function obtenerPedidosDelDia(repartidorId: string) {\n  const startOfDay = new Date();\n  startOfDay.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);\n  const endOfDay = new Date(startOfDay);\n  endOfDay.setDate(endOfDay.getDate() + 1);\n\n  const pedidos = await prisma.pedido.findMany({\n    where: {\n      reparto: { repartidorId },\n      fecha: { gte: startOfDay, lt: endOfDay },\n      deletedAt: null,\n    },\n    include: DETALLE_INCLUDE,\n    orderBy: { orden: 'asc' },\n  });\n\n  return pedidos.map(formatPedidoDetalle);\n}\n\n/** GET /pedidos/:id ÔÇö Obtener detalle completo de un pedido */\nexport async function obtenerPedido(id: string) {\n  const pedido = await prisma.pedido.findUnique({\n    where: { id },\n    include: DETALLE_INCLUDE,\n  });\n\n  if (!pedido || pedido.deletedAt) {\n    throw ApiError.notFound('Pedido no encontrado');\n  }\n\n  return formatPedidoDetalle(pedido);\n}\n\n/** GET /pedidos ÔÇö Listar pedidos con filtros y paginaci├│n */\nexport async function listarPedidos(params: {\n  clienteId?: string;\n  clienteNombre?: string;\n  estado?: string;\n  fechaDesde?: string;\n  fechaHasta?: string;\n  repartoId?: string;\n  page?: number;\n  pageSize?: number;\n}) {\n  const where: Record<string, unknown> = {\n    deletedAt: null,\n  };\n\n  if (params.estado) {\n    where['estado'] = params.estado;\n  }\n\n  if (params.clienteId) {\n    where['clienteId'] = params.clienteId;\n  } else if (params.clienteNombre) {\n    where['OR'] = [\n      { cliente: { nombre: { contains: params.clienteNombre, mode: 'insensitive' } } },\n      { cliente: { apellido: { contains: params.clienteNombre, mode: 'insensitive' } } },\n    ];\n  }\n\n  if (params.repartoId) {\n    where['repartoId'] = params.repartoId;\n  }\n\n  if (params.fechaDesde || params.fechaHasta) {\n    const fechaFilter: Record<string, Date> = {};\n    if (params.fechaDesde) {\n      fechaFilter['gte'] = new Date(params.fechaDesde);\n    }\n    if (params.fechaHasta) {\n      fechaFilter['lte'] = new Date(params.fechaHasta);\n    }\n    where['fecha'] = fechaFilter;\n  }\n\n  const page = params.page ?? 1;\n  const pageSize = params.pageSize ?? 20;\n  const skip = (page - 1) * pageSize;\n\n  const [pedidos, total] = await Promise.all([\n    prisma.pedido.findMany({\n      where,\n      include: DETALLE_INCLUDE,\n      orderBy: { orden: 'asc' },\n      skip,\n      take: pageSize,\n    }),\n    prisma.pedido.count({ where }),\n  ]);\n\n  return {\n    data: pedidos.map(formatPedidoResumen),\n    total,\n    page,\n    pageSize,\n  };\n}\n\n/** POST /pedidos ÔÇö Crear un nuevo pedido */\nexport async function crearPedido(data: {\n  clienteId: string;\n  repartoId?: string;\n  items: Array<{ itemId: string; cantidad: number }>;\n}) {\n  // Verificar que el cliente existe\n  const cliente = await prisma.cliente.findUnique({ where: { id: data.clienteId } });\n  if (!cliente) {\n    throw ApiError.notFound('Cliente no encontrado');\n  }\n\n  // Si se especific├│ reparto, verificar que existe\n  if (data.repartoId) {\n    const reparto = await prisma.reparto.findUnique({ where: { id: data.repartoId } });\n    if (!reparto) {\n      throw ApiError.notFound('Reparto no encontrado');\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Verificar que todos los items existen, est├ín activos y obtener sus precios\n  const itemsConPrecio: Array<{ itemId: string; cantidad: number; precioUnitario: number }> = [];\n  for (const item of data.items) {\n    const dbItem = await prisma.item.findUnique({ where: { id: item.itemId } });\n    if (!dbItem) {\n      throw ApiError.badRequest(`El ├¡tem ${item.itemId} no existe`);\n    }\n    if (!dbItem.activo) {\n      throw ApiError.badRequest(`El ├¡tem \"${dbItem.nombre}\" no est├í disponible`);\n    }\n    itemsConPrecio.push({\n      itemId: item.itemId,\n      cantidad: item.cantidad,\n      precioUnitario: dbItem.precio,\n    });\n  }\n\n  // Fecha actual como fecha del pedido si no se asigna a un reparto\n  const fecha = new Date();\n\n  // Determinar orden (siguiente disponible)\n  const maxOrden = await prisma.pedido.aggregate({ _max: { orden: true } });\n  const orden = (maxOrden._max.orden ?? 0) + 1;\n\n  const pedido = await prisma.pedido.create({\n    data: {\n      clienteId: data.clienteId,\n      repartoId: data.repartoId ?? null,\n      fecha,\n      estado: 'PENDIENTE',\n      orden,\n      items: {\n        create: itemsConPrecio.map((i) => ({\n          itemId: i.itemId,\n          cantidad: i.cantidad,\n          precioUnitario: i.precioUnitario,\n        })),\n      },\n    },\n    include: DETALLE_INCLUDE,\n  });\n\n  return formatPedidoDetalle(pedido);\n}\n\n// ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ State machine ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\nconst TRANSICIONES_VALIDAS: Record<string, string[]> = {\n  PENDIENTE: ['EN_RUTA'],\n  EN_RUTA: ['ENTREGADO', 'NO_ENTREGADO'],\n  ENTREGADO: [],\n  NO_ENTREGADO: [],\n  CANCELADO: [],\n};\n\nfunction validarTransicion(estadoActual: string, nuevoEstado: string): void {\n  const permitidos = TRANSICIONES_VALIDAS[estadoActual];\n  if (!permitidos || !permitidos.includes(nuevoEstado)) {\n    throw ApiError.conflict(\n      `No se puede cambiar de '${estadoActual}' a '${nuevoEstado}'`\n    );\n  }\n}\n\n/** PATCH /pedidos/:id/estado ÔÇö Actualizar estado del pedido (m├íquina de estados) */\nexport async function actualizarEstado(id: string, nuevoEstado: string) {\n  const pedido = await prisma.pedido.findUnique({ where: { id } });\n\n  if (!pedido || pedido.deletedAt) {\n    throw ApiError.notFound('Pedido no encontrado');\n  }\n\n  validarTransicion(pedido.estado, nuevoEstado);\n\n  const updated = await prisma.pedido.update({\n    where: { id },\n    data: { estado: nuevoEstado as EstadoPedido },\n    include: DETALLE_INCLUDE,\n  });\n\n  return formatPedidoDetalle(updated);\n}\n\n/** POST /pedidos/:id/cancelar ÔÇö Cancelar pedido (solo desde PENDIENTE) */\nexport async function cancelarPedido(id: string) {\n  const pedido = await prisma.pedido.findUnique({ where: { id } });\n\n  if (!pedido || pedido.deletedAt) {\n    throw ApiError.notFound('Pedido prisma.pedido.update({\n    where: { id },\n    data: { estado: 'CANCELADO' },\n    include: DETALLE_INCLUDE,\n  });\n\n  return formatPedidoDetalle(updated);\n}\n\n/** PATCH /pedidos/:id/confirmar ÔÇö Confirmar entrega (backward compat) */\nexport async function confirmarEntrega(id: string) {\n  const pedido = await prisma.pedido.findUnique({ where: { id } });\n\n  if (!pedido || pedido.deletedAt) {\n    throw ApiError.notFound('Pedido no encontrado');\n  }\n\n  // Permitir desde PENDIENTE (backward compat) o EN_RUTA\n  if (pedido.estado !== 'PENDIENTE' && pedido.estado !== 'EN_RUTA') {\n    throw ApiError.conflict('El pedido no puede ser entregado desde su estado actual');\n  }\n\n  const updated = await prisma.pedido.update({\n    where: { id },\n    data: { estado: 'ENTREGADO' },\n    include: DETALLE_INCLUDE,\n  });\n\n  return formatPedidoDetalle(updated);\n}\n\n/** PATCH /pedidos/:id/cancelar (repartidor) ÔÇö Marcar como NO_ENTREGADO (backward compat) */\nexport async function cancelarPedidoRepartidor(id: string, motivo: string) {\n  const pedido = await prisma.pedido.findUnique({ where: { id } });\n\n  if (!pedido || pedido.deletedAt) {\n    throw ApiError.notFound('Pedido no encontrado');\n  }\n\n  if (pedido.estado !== 'EN_RUTA' && pedido.estado !== 'PENDIENTE') {\n    throw ApiError.conflict('El pedido no puede marcarse como no entregado });\n\n  return formatPedidoDetalle(updated);\n}\n\n/** DELETE /pedidos/:id ÔÇö Soft delete */\nexport async function eliminarPedido(id: string) {\n  const pedido = await prisma.pedido.findUnique({ where: { id } });\n\n  if (!pedido || pedido.deletedAt) {\n    throw ApiError.notFound('Pedido no encontrado');\n  }\n\n  if (pedido.estado !== 'PENDIENTE' && pedido.estado !== 'CANCELADO') {\n pedidoId },\n    include: DETALLE_INCLUDE,\n  });\n\n  if (!pedido || pedido.deletedAt) {\n    throw ApiError.notFound('Pedido no encontrado');\n  }\n\n  if (pedido.estado !== 'PENDIENTE') {\n    throw ApiError.conflict(\n      'Solo se pueden modificar pedidos en estado pendiente'\n    );\n  }\n\n  return pedido;\n}\n\n/** POST /pedidos/:pedidoId/items ÔÇö Agregar item a pedido */\nexport async function agregarItem(\n  pedidoId: string,\n  data: { itemId: string; cantidad: number }\n) {\n  await verificarPedidoPendiente(pedidoId);\n\n  // Verificar que el item existe y est├í activo\n  const dbItem = await prisma.item.findUnique({ where: { id: data.itemId } });\n  if (!dbItem) {\n    throw ApiError.badRequest('El ├¡tem no existe');\n  }\n  if (!dbItem.activo) {\n    throw ApiError.badRequest(`El ├¡tem \"${dbItem.nombre}\" no est├í disponible`);\n  }\n\n  // Verificar que el item no est├® ya en el pedido\n  const existente = await prisma.pedidoItem.findFirst({\n    where: { pedidoId, itemId: data.itemId },\n  });\n  if (existente) {\n    throw ApiError.conflict('El ├¡tem ya existe en el pedido. data.cantidad,\n      precioUnitario: dbItem.precio,\n    },\n    include: { item: true },\n  });\n\n  // Devolver el pedido actualizado\n  const pedido = await prisma.pedido.findUnique({\n    where: { id: pedidoId },\n    include: DETALLE_INCLUDE,\n  });\n\n  return formatPedidoDetalle(pedido!);\n}\n\n/** PATCH /pedidos/:pedidoId/items/:itemId ÔÇö Actualizar cantidad de item */\nexport async function actualizarCantidadItem(\n  pedidoId: string,\n  itemId: string,\n  cantidad: number\n) {\n  await verificarPedidoPendiente(pedidoId);\n\n  const itemExistente = await prisma.pedidoItem.findFirst({\n    where: { id: itemId, pedidoId },\n  });\n  if (!itemExistente) {\n    throw ApiError.notFound('El ├¡tem no existe en el pedido');\n  }\n\n  await DETALLE_INCLUDE,\n  });\n\n  return formatPedidoDetalle(pedido!);\n}\n\n/** DELETE /pedidos/:pedidoId/items/:itemId ÔÇö Quitar item del pedido */\nexport async function quitarItem(pedidoId: string, import { Router } from 'express';\nimport {\n  obtenerHoyController,\n  obtenerController,\n  listarController,\n  crearController,\n  actualizarEstadoController,\n  cancelarController,\n  eliminarController,\n  agregarItemController,\n  actualizarCantidadItemController,\n  quitarItemController,\n  confirmarController,\n  cancelarRepartidorController,\n} from './controller.js';\nimport { authenticate, requireRole } from '../../middleware/auth.middleware.js';\n\nconst router = Router();\n\n// ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ Rutas p├║blicas (autenticadas) ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\n// TDD-0032: Obtener detalle de pedido\nrouter.get('/:id', authenticate, obtenerController);\n\n// TDD-0033: Listar pedidos con filtros y paginaci├│n\nrouter.get('/', authenticate, listarController);\n\n// TDD-0031: Crear pedido (solo ADMIN)\nrouter.post('/', authenticate, requireRole('ADMIN'), crearController);\n\n// TDD-0034: Actualizar estado (ADMIN o REPARTIDOR)\nrouter.patch('/:id/estado', authenticate, actualizarEstadoController);\n\n// TDD-0035: ### Contenido:

'../../../middleware/error-handler.js';\n\n// ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ Mock prisma ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\nconst mockPrisma = {\n  pedido: {\n    findMany: vi.fn(),\n    findUnique: vi.fn(),\n    findFirst: vi.fn(),\n    count: vi.fn(),\n    update: vi.fn(),\n    create: vi.fn(),\n    aggregate: vi.fn(),\n  },\n  cliente: { findUnique: vi.fn() },\n  reparto: { findUnique: vi.fn() },\n  item: { findUnique: vi.fn() },\n  pedidoItem: {\n    findFirst: vi.fn(),\n    count: vi.fn(),\n    create: vi.fn(),\n    update: vi.fn(),\n    delete: vi.fn(),\n  },\n};\n\nvi.mock('../../../lib/prisma.js', () => ({ prisma: mockPrisma }));\n\n// ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ Helpers ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\nconst JWT_SECRET = 'supplycycle-dev-secret';\n\nfunction buildToken(overrides: Record<string, unknown> = {}) {\n  return jwt.sign(\n    { userId: 'usr-001', email: 'admin@test.com', rol: 'ADMIN', ...overrides },\n    JWT_SECRET,\n    { expiresIn: '1h' }\n  );\n}\n\nfunction buildRepartidorToken() {\n  return buildToken({ userId: 'usr-002', email: 'repartidor@test.com', rol: 'REPARTIDOR' });\n}\n\nfunction buildMockPedido(overrides: Record<string, unknown> = {}) {\n  const now = new Date('2026-05-22T10:00:00Z');\n  return {\n    id: 'ped-001',\n    orden: 1,\n    estado: 'PENDIENTE',\n    fecha: now,\n    creadoEn: now,\n    actualizadoEn: now,\n    deletedAt: null,\n    motivoFalla: null,\n    clienteId: 'cli-001',\n    repartoId: 'rep-001',\n    cliente: {\n      id: 'cli-001',\n      nombre: 'Juan',\n      apellido: 'P├®rez',\n      telefono: '1145678901',\n      calle: 'Av. Corrientes',\n      numero: '1234',\n      localidad: 'CABA',\n      latitud: -34.6037,\n      longitud: -58.3816,\n      horarioDesde: '09:00',\n      horarioHasta: '11:00',\n    },\n    reparto: { id: 'rep-001', fecha: now },\n    items: [\n      {\n        id: 'item-ped-001',\n        cantidad: 2,\n        precioUnitario: 1500,\n        item: {\n          id: 'prod-001',\n          nombre: 'Bid├│n 20L',\n          descripcion: null,\n          precio: 1500,\n          unidad: 'unidad',\n          activo: true,\n        },\n      },\n    ],\n    ...overrides,\n  };\n}\n\n// ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ Setup app ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\nasync function createApp() {\n  const { default: pedidosRoutes } = await import('../routes.js');\n  const app = express();\n  app.use(express.json());\n  app.use('/api/v1/pedidos', pedidosRoutes);\n  app.use(errorHandler);\n  return app;\n}\n\n// ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ Tests ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\ndescribe('Pedidos Routes', () => {\n  let app: express.Express;\n  let adminToken: string;\n  let repartidorToken: string;\n\n  beforeEach(async () => {\n    vi.clearAllMocks();\n    app = await createApp();\n    adminToken = buildToken();\n    repartidorToken = buildRepartidorToken();\n  });\n\n  // ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ TDD-0031: POST /api/v1/pedidos ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\n  describe('POST /api/v1/pedidos (TDD-0031)', () => {\n    it('debe crear un pedido (201)', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.cliente.findUnique.mockResolvedValue({ id: 'cli-001', nombre: 'Juan' });\n      mockPrisma.item.findUnique.mockResolvedValue({ id: 'prod-001', nombre: 'Bid├│n 20L', precio: 1500, activo: true });\n      mockPrisma.pedido.aggregate.mockResolvedValue({ _max: { orden: 5 } });\n      mockPrisma.pedido.create.mockResolvedValue(buildMockPedido());\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .post('/api/v1/pedidos')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`)\n        .send({ clienteId: 'cli-001', items: [{ itemId: 'prod-001', cantidad: 2 }] });\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(201);\n      expect(res.body.data).toBeDefined();\n      expect(res.body.data.id).toBe('ped-001');\n      expect(res.body.data.estado).toBe('PENDIENTE');\n    });\n\n    it('debe retornar 401 sin token', async () => {\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .post('/api/v1/pedidos')\n        .send({ clienteId: 'cli-001', items: [] });\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(401);\n    });\n\n    it('debe retornar 403 si es REPARTIDOR', async () => {\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .post('/api/v1/pedidos')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${repartidorToken}`)\n        .send({ clienteId: 'cli-001', items: [{ itemId: 'prod-001', cantidad: 2 }] });\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(403);\n    });\n\n    it('debe retornar 400 si el body es inv├ílido', async () => {\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .post('/api/v1/pedidos')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`)\n        .send({ clienteId: 'invalid-uuid', items: [] });\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(400);\n    });\n  });\n\n  // ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ TDD-0032: GET /api/v1/pedidos/:id ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\n  describe('GET /api/v1/pedidos/:id (TDD-0032)', () => {\n    it('debe retornar el detalle del pedido (200)', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findUnique.mockResolvedValue(buildMockPedido());\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .get('/api/v1/pedidos/ped-001')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`);\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(200);\n      expect(res.body.data.id).toBe('ped-001');\n      expect(res.body.data.cliente.nombre).toBe('Juan P├®rez');\n      expect(res.body.data.total).toBe(3000);\n    });\n\n    it('debe retornar 404 si no existe', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findUnique.mockResolvedValue(null);\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .get('/api/v1/pedidos/ped-999')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`);\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(404);\n    });\n  });\n\n  // ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ TDD-0033: GET /api/v1/pedidos ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\n  describe('GET /api/v1/pedidos (TDD-0033)', () => {\n    it('debe retornar lista paginada (200)', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findMany.mockResolvedValue([buildMockPedido()]);\n      mockPrisma.pedido.count.mockResolvedValue(1);\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .get('/api/v1/pedidos')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`);\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(200);\n      expect(res.body.data).toHaveLength(1);\n      expect(res.body.total).toBe(1);\n      expect(res.body.page).toBe(1);\n      expect(res.body.pageSize).toBe(20);\n    });\n\n    it('debe filtrar por estado', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findMany.mockResolvedValue([]);\n      mockPrisma.pedido.count.mockResolvedValue(0);\n\n      await request(app)\n        .get('/api/v1/pedidos?estado=ENTREGADO')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`);\n\n      expect(mockPrisma.pedido.findMany).toHaveBeenCalledWith(\n        expect.objectContaining({\n          where: expect.objectContaining({ estado: 'ENTREGADO' }),\n        })\n      );\n    });\n  });\n\n  // ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ TDD-0034: PATCH /api/v1/pedidos/:id/estado ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\n  describe('PATCH /api/v1/pedidos/:id/estado (TDD-0034)', () => {\n    it('debe actualizar estado correctamente (200)', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findUnique.mockResolvedValue(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'PENDIENTE' }));\n      mockPrisma.pedido.update.mockResolvedValue(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'EN_RUTA' }));\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .patch('/api/v1/pedidos/ped-001/estado')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`)\n        .send({ estado: 'EN_RUTA' });\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(200);\n      expect(res.body.data.estado).toBe('EN_RUTA');\n    });\n\n    it('debe rechazar transici├│n inv├ílida (409)', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findUnique.mockResolvedValue(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'ENTREGADO' }));\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .patch('/api/v1/pedidos/ped-001/estado')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`)\n        .send({ estado: 'EN_RUTA' });\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(409);\n    });\n\n    it('debe permitir a REPARTIDOR cambiar estado (200)', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findUnique.mockResolvedValue(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'EN_RUTA' }));\n      mockPrisma.pedido.update.mockResolvedValue(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'ENTREGADO' }));\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .patch('/api/v1/pedidos/ped-001/estado')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${repartidorToken}`)\n        .send({ estado: 'ENTREGADO' });\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(200);\n    });\n  });\n\n  // ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ TDD-0035: POST /api/v1/pedidos/:id/cancelar ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\n  describe('POST /api/v1/pedidos/:id/cancelar (TDD-0035)', () => {\n    it('debe cancelar un pedido pendiente (200)', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findUnique.mockResolvedValue(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'PENDIENTE' }));\n      mockPrisma.pedido.update.mockResolvedValue(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'CANCELADO' }));\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .post('/api/v1/pedidos/ped-001/cancelar')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`);\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(200);\n      expect(res.body.data.estado).toBe('CANCELADO');\n    });\n\n    it('debe retornar 403 si es REPARTIDOR', async () => {\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .post('/api/v1/pedidos/ped-001/cancelar')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${repartidorToken}`);\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(403);\n    });\n  });\n\n  // ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ TDD-0036: DELETE /api/v1/pedidos/:id ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\n  describe('DELETE /api/v1/pedidos/:id (TDD-0036)', () => {\n    it('debe eliminar (soft delete) un pedido pendiente (200)', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findUnique.mockResolvedValue(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'PENDIENTE' }));\n      mockPrisma.pedido.update.mockResolvedValue(\n        buildMockPedido({ estado: 'PENDIENTE', deletedAt: new Date() })\n      );\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .delete('/api/v1/pedidos/ped-001')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`);\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(200);\n      expect(res.body.data.id).toBe('ped-001');\n    });\n\n    it('debe retornar 409 si est├í EN_RUTA', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findUnique.mockResolvedValue(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'EN_RUTA' }));\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .delete('/api/v1/pedidos/ped-001')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`);\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(409);\n    });\n  });\n\n  // ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ TDD-0037: POST /api/v1/pedidos/:pedidoId/items ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\n  describe('POST /api/v1/pedidos/:pedidoId/items (TDD-0037)', () => {\n    it('debe agregar un item al pedido (201)', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findUnique\n        .mockResolvedValueOnce(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'PENDIENTE' })) // verificarPedidoPendiente\n        .mockResolvedValueOnce(buildMockPedido({ // re-fetch after create (dentro de agregarItem)\n          items: [\n            buildMockPedido().items[0]!,\n            { id: 'new-item', cantidad: 3, precioUnitario: 900, item: { id: 'prod-002', nombre: 'Bid├│n 12L', descripcion: null, precio: 900, unidad: 'unidad', activo: true } },\n          ],\n        }));\n      mockPrisma.item.findUnique.mockResolvedValue({ id: 'prod-002', nombre: 'Bid├│n 12L', precio: 900, activo: true });\n      mockPrisma.pedidoItem.findFirst.mockResolvedValue(null);\n      mockPrisma.pedidoItem.create.mockResolvedValue({});\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .post('/api/v1/pedidos/ped-001/items')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`)\n        .send({ itemId: 'prod-002', cantidad: 3 });\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(201);\n      expect(res.body.data).toBeDefined();\n    });\n  });\n\n  // ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ TDD-0038: PATCH /api/v1/pedidos/:pedidoId/items/:itemId ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\n  describe('PATCH /api/v1/pedidos/:pedidoId/items/:itemId (TDD-0038)', () => {\n    it('debe actualizar la cantidad (200)', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findUnique\n        .mockResolvedValueOnce(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'PENDIENTE' }))\n        .mockResolvedValueOnce(buildMockPedido());\n      mockPrisma.pedidoItem.findFirst.mockResolvedValue({ id: 'item-ped-001', pedidoId: 'ped-001' });\n      mockPrisma.pedidoItem.update.mockResolvedValue({});\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .patch('/api/v1/pedidos/ped-001/items/item-ped-001')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`)\n        .send({ cantidad: 5 });\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(200);\n    });\n  });\n\n  // ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ TDD-0039: DELETE /api/v1/pedidos/:pedidoId/items/:itemId ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\n  describe('DELETE /api/v1/pedidos/:pedidoId/items/:itemId (TDD-0039)', () => {\n    it('debe quitar un item del pedido (200)', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findUnique\n        .mockResolvedValueOnce(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'PENDIENTE' }))\n        .mockResolvedValueOnce(buildMockPedido({ items: [] }));\n      mockPrisma.pedidoItem.findFirst.mockResolvedValue({ id: 'item-ped-001', pedidoId: 'ped-001' });\n      mockPrisma.pedidoItem.count.mockResolvedValue(2);\n      mockPrisma.pedidoItem.delete.mockResolvedValue({});\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .delete('/api/v1/pedidos/ped-001/items/item-ped-001')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`);\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(200);\n    });\n\n    it('debe retornar 409 si es el ├║ltimo item', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findUnique.mockResolvedValue(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'PENDIENTE' }));\n      mockPrisma.pedidoItem.findFirst.mockResolvedValue({ id: 'item-ped-001', pedidoId: 'ped-001' });\n      mockPrisma.pedidoItem.count.mockResolvedValue(1);\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .delete('/api/v1/pedidos/ped-001/items/item-ped-001')\n        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${adminToken}`);\n\n      expect(res.status).toBe(409);\n    });\n  });\n\n  // ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ Legacy: PATCH /:id/confirmar ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ\n\n  describe('PATCH /api/v1/pedidos/:id/confirmar (legacy)', () => {\n    it('debe confirmar entrega (200)', async () => {\n      mockPrisma.pedido.findUnique.mockResolvedValue(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'EN_RUTA' }));\n      mockPrisma.pedido.update.mockResolvedValue(buildMockPedido({ estado: 'ENTREGADO' }));\n\n      const res = await request(app)\n        .patch('/api/v1/pedidos/ped-001/confirmar')\n ### Mensaje:
The error says:\n1. `clienteId` - \"clienteId debe ser un UUID v├ílido\" \n2. `items.0.itemId` - \"itemId debe ser un UUID v├ílido\"\n\nSo the UUID constants are not being recognized as valid UUIDs by Zod! Let me check:\n- UUID.CLIENTE_001 = 'b0000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000001'\n- UUID.PROD_001 = 'd0000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000001'\n\nHmm, wait. The issue is that in Zod 4, the `uuid()` validator might require a specific UUID version (v4 specifically?). Let me check...\n\nIn Zod 4, `z.string().uuid()` validates that the string is a valid UUID. The standard UUID format is: 8-4-4-4-12 hex digits: `xxxxxxxx-xxxx-xxxx-xxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx`.\n\nMy UUIDs are: `b0000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000001` - this looks like a valid UUID format to me. 8-4-4-4-12 hex digits, all hex characters.\n\nWait, but maybe Zod 4 has a stricter validator? Let me check if Zod 4's uuid() requires UUID v4 specifically (with the version nibble being 4 in the 13th character position).\n\nActually, looking at the v4 UUID spec, the 13th character (the version nibble) should be '4' for UUID v4. import { apiClient } from '@/services/api';\nimport type { Pedido, EstadoPedido, MotivoCancelacion } from '@/types/pedido';\n\n/* ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ TDD-0032: Obtener detalle de pedido ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ */\n\nexport async function getPedidoByIdRequest(id: string): Promise<Pedido> {\n  const response = await apiClient.get<{ data: Pedido }>(`/pedidos/${id}`);\n  return response.data.data;\n}\n\n/* ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ TDD-0033: Listar pedidos con filtros ÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇÔöÇ */\n\nexport interface BuscarPedidosParams {\n  clienteId?: string;\n  clienteNombre?: string;\n android: `geo:0,0?q=${lat},${lng}`,\n      default: `https://www.google.com/maps?q=${lat},${lng}`,\n    });\n    if (url) Linking.openURL(url);\n  };\n\n  const handleConfirmar = () => {\n    confirmarMutation.mutate(id, {\n      onSuccess: () => {\n        router.back();\n      },\n    });\n  };\n\n  const handleCancelar = (motivo: MotivoCancelacion) => {\n    cancelarMutation.mutate(\n      { pedidoId: id, motivo },\n      {\n        onSuccess: () => {\n          setShowCancelModal(false);\n          router.back();\n        },\n      }\n    );\n  };\n\n  if (isLoading) {\n    return (\n      <ThemedView style={styles.container}>\n        <Header />\n        <LoadingSpinner message=\"Cargando detalle del pedido...\" />\n      </ThemedView>\n    );\n  }\n\n  if (isError || !pedido) {\n    return (\n      <ThemedView style={styles.container}>\n        <Header />\n        <ErrorMessage\n          message={error?.message || 'Error al cargar el pedido'}\n          onRetry={() => router.back()}\n        />\n      </ThemedView>\n    );\n  }\n\n  const isPending = pedido.estado === 'PENDIENTE';\n  const isEnRuta = pedido.estado === 'EN_RUTA';\n  const isTerminal =\n    pedido.estado === 'ENTREGADO' ||\n    pedido.estado === 'NO_ENTREGADO' ||\n    pedido.estado === 'CANCELADO';\n\n  return (\n    <ThemedView style={styles.container}>\n      <Header />\n      <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={styles.scrollContent}>\n        {/* Estado y total */}\n        <View style={styles.estadoContainer}>\n          <View\n            style={[\n              styles.estadoBadge,\n              {\n                backgroundColor: getEstadoColor(pedido.estado, theme) + '20',\n              },\n            ]}\n          >\n            <Text\n              style={[\n                styles.estadoText,\n                { color: getEstadoColor(pedido.estado, theme) },\n              ]}\n            >\n              {getEstadoLabel(pedido.estado)}\n            </Text>\n          </View>\n          <View style={styles.estadoRight}>\n            <Text style={[styles.ordenText, { color: theme.muted }]}>\n              Pedido #{pedido.orden}\n            </Text>\n            {pedido.total !== undefined && pedido.total !== null && (\n              <Text style={[styles.totalText, { color: theme.text }]}>\n                {formatCurrency(pedido.total)}\n              </Text>\n            )}\n          </View>\n        </View>\n\n        {/* Fecha de alta */}\n        {pedido.fechaAlta && (\n          <Text style={[styles.fechaAltaText, { color: theme.muted }]}>\n            Creado: {formatFecha(pedido.fechaAlta)}\n          </Text>\n        )}\n\n        {/* Reparto asignado */}\n        {pedido.reparto && (\n          <Text style={[styles.repartoText, { color: theme.info }]}>\n            Reparto: {formatFecha(pedido.reparto.fecha)}\n          </Text>\n        )}\n\n        {/* Cliente */}\n        <Card>\n          <Text style={[styles.clienteNombre, { color: theme.text }]}>\n            {pedido.cliente.nombre} {pedido.cliente.apellido}\n          </Text>\n\n          <TouchableOpacity\n            style={styles.infoRow}\n            onPress={() =>\n              handleOpenMaps(\n                pedido.cliente.domicilio.latitud,\n                pedido.cliente.domicilio.longitud\n              )\n            }\n          >\n            <Text style={[styles.infoLabel, { color: theme.muted }]}>\n              Direcci├│n\n            </Text>\n            <Text style={[styles.infoValue, { Even though `/repartos/[id]` exists as a route, the template literal `` `/repartos/${pedido.id}` `` produces a type of `` `/repartos/${string}` `` which the TypeScript type system can't statically verify matches the known route pattern.\n\nThe fix is to use the object form:\n\n```ts\nrouter.push({ pathname: '/repartos/[id]', params: { id: pedido.id } })\n```\n\nThis is the standard Expo Router 6 way to navigate programmatically to dynamic routes.\n\nNow let me also check `app/(tabs)/pedidos/` to see if `[id].tsx` exists.\n\nWait, the glob result confirmed: no `app/(tabs)/pedidos/[id].tsx` file exists. prev.filter((s) => s.item.id !== item.id);\n        }\n        return [...prev, { item, cantidad: 1 }];\n      });\n    },\n    []\n  );\n\n  const updateCantidad = useCallback(\n    (itemId: string, return { ...s, cantidad: nueva };\n        })\n      );\n    },\n    []\n  );\n\n  const totalEstimado = selectedItems.reduce(\n    (sum, s) => sum + (s.item.precio ?? 0) * s.cantidad,\n    0\n  );\n\n  const handleSubmit = useCallback(() => {\n    if (!selectedCliente) {\n      Alert.alert('Faltan datos', 'Seleccion├í un cliente para el pedido');\n      return;\n    }\n    if repartoId: selectedReparto?.id ?? undefined,\n      items: selectedItems.map((s) => ({\n        itemId: s.item.id,\n        cantidad: s.cantidad,\n      })),\n    };\n\n    crearPedido.mutate(payload, The `useCrearPedido` hook doesn't actually have a mock fallback in the mutationFn itself. Since mutations are different from queries, and the onError just has an empty comment, I should improve this. If the backend is not available, the mutation will fail and show an error to the user via the Alert.\n\nHowever, looking at how the other hooks work, they use try/catch in the queryFn with a mock fallback. For a mutation, this is trickier because the mutation itself needs to succeed for the UI state to update correctly. But since the mock data won't actually create a real pedido on the backend, it's fine to just let it hit the real API and show an error if it fails.\n\nActually, let me think about this more carefully. This is correct!\n\nSimilarly for items:\n```ts\nconst response = await apiClient.get<{ data: Item[] }>('/items');\nreturn response.data.data;\n```\n\nThis is also correct.\n\nNow let me think about what else could be wrong...\n\nWait, the user said \"No funciona Get, Post\". Let me check if there's a problem with the `useBuscarPedidos` hook when it comes to the pedidos list page. \n\nLooking at `PedidosListScreen.tsx`:\n```tsx\nconst { data, isLoading, isError, error } = useBuscarPedidos({\n    clienteNombre: search || undefined,\n    estado: filtroEstado,\n});\n```\n\nThe `useBuscarPedidos` hook:\n```tsx\nexport function useBuscarPedidos(params?: BuscarPedidosParams) {\n  return useQuery<BuscarPedidosResponse>({\n    queryKey: ['pedidos', 'buscar', params],\n    queryFn: async () => {\n      try {\n        return await getPedidosRequest(params);\n      } catch {\n        const fallback = await mockGetPedidosRequest(params);\n        return { data: fallback.data, total: fallback.total, page: 1, pageSize: 20 };\n      }\n    },\n    staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000,\n  });\n}\n```\n\n`getPedidosRequest` calls `apiClient.get<BuscarPedidosResponse>('/pedidos', { params })`.\n\nThe backend `listarController` parses query params and calls `listarPedidos`.\n\nNow, the `queryKey` includes `params` which is an object `{ clienteNombre, estado }`. When `search` changes (user types), the `params` object reference changes, so `useQuery` will re-fetch. This should work correctly.\n\nBut wait, there's a subtle issue with `queryKey: ['pedidos', 'buscar', params]`. The `params` is an object `{ clienteNombre: string | undefined, estado: EstadoPedido | undefined }`. When the user hasn't typed anything and hasn't selected a state, `params` is `{}` (empty). When the user types \"foo\", `params` is `{ clienteNombre: 'foo', estado: undefined }`.\n\nTanStack Query uses referential equality for query keys. Since `params` is a new object each render, even if the values are the same, the query key will be different. This means the query will be re-fetched on every render.\n\nBut this is a performance issue, not a \"doesn't work\" issue.\n\nActually, looking more carefully, the `useBuscarPedidos` is called with inline params:\n```tsx\nconst { data, isLoading, isError, error } = useBuscarPedidos({\n    clienteNombre: search || undefined,\n    estado: filtroEstado,\n});\n```\n\nSince `search` is a string state variable, it only changes on user input. So re-renders happen when the search text changes, which is fine.\n\nOK let me think about what ELSE could be wrong...\n\nActually, wait. Let me think about the auth flow one more time:\n\n1. User opens app ÔåÆ `_layout.tsx` bootstrap runs\n2. Token is in SecureStore ÔåÆ tries `GET /api/v1/auth/me` with `fetch`\n3. If backend not running ÔåÆ catch ÔåÆ mock fallback ÔåÆ shows tabs\n\nNow, the `fetch` call in `_layout.tsx` uses `fetch` not `apiClient`. The `fetch` call doesn't go through the Axios interceptor. So:\n- If the backend returns 401 (invalid token), `response.ok` is false\n- The code falls through to the mock fallback (no mock token handling)\n\nBut actually looking at the code more carefully:\n```ts\nconst response = await fetch(`${EXPO_PUBLIC_API_URL}/auth/me`, { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` } });\nif (response.ok) {\n    const usuario = await response.json();\n    setAuth(token, usuario);\n    return;\n}\n```\n\nIf `response.ok` is false, nothing happens (no `return`), so execution continues to the mock fallback:\n```ts\nconst { mockGetMeRequest } = await import('@/features/auth/services/mockAuthService');\nconst usuario = await mockGetMeRequest();\nsetAuth(token, usuario);\n```\n\nSo even with a real backend running, if the token is invalid, the mock fallback is used. But the mock token is stored, and subsequent API calls will fail.\n\nThis is actually the design pattern ÔÇö the app uses mock data when the backend is not available. When the user logs in with real credentials on a real backend, a real JWT is returned and used for all subsequent API calls.\n\nOK, I think the core issue the user reported is fixed now:\n1. `producto` ÔåÆ `item` (backend format matches mobile type)\n2. `formatPedidoResumen` includes full cliente (list view works)\n3. Backend returns `{ token: \"real-jwt\", usuario: { ... } }`\n3. `loginRequest` returns `response.data` = `{ token, usuario }`\n4. `saveToken(data.token)` saves the real JWT\n5. `setAuth(data.token, data.usuario)` updates the store\n\nNow subsequent API calls use the real JWT via the request interceptor.\n\nThis should work correctly. ### Contenido:
import { create } from 'zustand';\n\nexport interface ApiCallRecord {\n  method: string;\n  url: string;\n  status: number;\n  statusText: string;\n  timestamp: number;\n  success: boolean;\n}\n\ninterface ApiStatusState {\n  /** ├Ültima respuesta registrada (├║til para mostrar en UI) */\n  lastCall: ApiCallRecord | null;\n  /** Historial de las ├║ltimas N llamadas */\n  history: ApiCallRecord[];\n  /** Registrar una nueva respuesta */\n  recordCall: (call: ApiCallRecord) => void;\n  /** Limpiar el historial */\n  clearHistory: () => void;\n}\n\nconst MAX_HISTORY = 20;\n\nexport const useApiStatusStore = create<ApiStatusState>((set) => ({\n  lastCall: null,\n  history: [],\n  recordCall: (call) =>\n    set((state) => ({\n      lastCall: call,\n      history: [call, ...state.history].slice(0, MAX_HISTORY),\n    })),\n  clearHistory: () => set({ lastCall: null, history: [] }),\n}));\n

import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';\nimport { Animated, StyleSheet, Text, TouchableOpacity, View } from 'react-native';\nimport { useApiStatusStore } from '@/stores/apiStatusStore';\nimport { useColorScheme } from '@/hooks/use-color-scheme';\nimport { Colors, Spacing, FontSizes, BorderRadius } from '@/constants/theme';\n\nconst AUTO_HIDE_MS = 4000;\n\nexport default function ApiStatusBanner() {\n  const colorScheme = useColorScheme() ?? 'light';\n  const theme = Colors[colorScheme];\n  const lastCall = useApiStatusStore((s) => s.lastCall);\n  const [visible, setVisible] = useState(false);\n\n  const opacity = useRef(new Animated.Value(0)).current;\n  const timerRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!lastCall) return;\n\n    // Cancelar ocultamiento pendiente\n    if (timerRef.current) clearTimeout(timerRef.current);\n\n    // Mostrar\n    setVisible(true);\n    Animated.timing(opacity, {\n      toValue: 1,\n      duration: 200,\n      useNativeDriver: true,\n    }).start();\n\n    // Ocultar despu├®s de N segundos\n    timerRef.current = setTimeout(() => {\n      Animated.timing(opacity, {\n        toValue: 0,\n        duration: 300,\n        useNativeDriver: true,\n      }).start(() => setVisible(false));\n    }, AUTO_HIDE_MS);\n\n    return () => {\n      if (timerRef.current) clearTimeout(timerRef.current);\n    };\n  }, [lastCall, opacity]);\n\n  if (!visible || !lastCall) return null;\n\n  const isSuccess = lastCall.success;\n  const bgColor = isSuccess ? theme.success : theme.error;\n\n  return (\n    <Animated.View\n      style={[styles.container, { opacity, backgroundColor: bgColor }]}\n    >\n      <TouchableOpacity\n        activeOpacity={0.8}\n        onPress={() => {\n          // Tocar para ver historial completo (m├ís adelante)\n          Animated.timing(opacity, {\n            toValue: 0,\n            duration: 200,\n            useNativeDriver: true,\n          }).start(() => setVisible(false));\n        }}\n        style={styles.inner}\n      >\n        <Text style={styles.method}>{lastCall.method}</Text>\n        <Text style={styles.url} numberOfLines={1}>\n          {lastCall.url}\n        </Text>\n        <View style={styles.statusBadge}>\n          <Text style={styles.statusText}>\n            {lastCall.status} {lastCall.statusText}\n          </Text>\n        </View>\n      </TouchableOpacity>\n    </Animated.View>\n  );\n}\n\nconst styles = StyleSheet.create({\n  container: {\n    position: 'absolute',\n    bottom: 100, // por encima de la tab bar\n    left: Spacing.lg,\n    right: Spacing.lg,\n    borderRadius: BorderRadius.md,\n    elevation: 8,\n    shadowColor: '#000',\n    shadowOffset: { width: 0, height: 2 },\n    shadowOpacity: 0.25,\n    shadowRadius: 4,\n    zIndex: 9999,\n  },\n  inner: {\n    flexDirection: 'row',\n    alignItems: 'center',\n    paddingVertical: Spacing.sm,\n    paddingHorizontal: Spacing.md,\n    gap: Spacing.sm,\n  },\n  method: {\n    color: '#FFFFFF',\n    fontSize: FontSizes.xs,\n    fontWeight: '800',\n    fontFamily: 'monospace',\n    backgroundColor: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)',\n    paddingHorizontal: 6,\n    paddingVertical: 2,\n    borderRadius: 4,\n    overflow: 'hidden',\n  },\n  url: {\n    color: '#FFFFFF',\n    fontSize: FontSizes.xs,\n    fontWeight: '600',\n    flex: 1,\n  },\n  statusBadge: {\n    backgroundColor: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.25)',\n    paddingHorizontal: 6,\n    paddingVertical: 2,\n    borderRadius: 4,\n  },\n  statusText: {\n    color: '#FFFFFF',\n    fontSize: FontSizes.xs,\n    fontWeight: '700',\n    fontFamily: 'monospace',\n  },\n});\n

## Resumen\n\nSe implement├│ un sistema global que muestra el c├│digo de respuesta HTTP de **cada petici├│n** al backend en un banner flotante en la pantalla.\n\n### Archivos creados\n\n| Archivo | Prop├│sito |\n|---|---|\n| `stores/apiStatusStore.ts` | Store Zustand que registra cada llamada API (`method`, `url`, `status`, `statusText`, `timestamp`, `success`) y mantiene un historial de las ├║ltimas 20 |\n| `components/ui/ApiStatusBanner.tsx` | Banner flotante en la parte inferior de la pantalla que se muestra autom├íticamente tras cada respuesta |\n\n### Archivos modificados\n\n| Archivo | Cambio |\n|---|---|\n| `services/api.ts` | Interceptor de respuesta modificado para **ambos casos** (├®xito y error): registra el m├®todo, URL, c├│digo HTTP y mensaje en la store. Adem├ís, los errores de red tambi├®n se registran con c├│digo `0` |\n| `app/_layout.tsx` | Se agreg├│ `<ApiStatusBanner />` despu├®s del Stack, visible en toda la app |\n| `components/ui/index.ts` | Exportado `ApiStatusBanner` |\n\n### C├│mo funciona\n\n1. **Cada respuesta** que pasa por Axios (interceptor) se registra autom├íticamente en `apiStatusStore`\n2. El **banner** escucha cambios en la store: cuando hay una nueva respuesta, aparece animado\n3. Muestra: `GET /pedidos ÔåÆ 200 OK` (verde) o `POST /pedidos ÔåÆ 500 Error interno` (rojo)\n4. Se **oculta solo** despu├®s de 4 segundos\n5. Se puede **descartar tocando** el banner\n6. Si hay un **error de red** (el servidor no responde), muestra `GET /pedidos ÔåÆ 0 Network Error`\n7. El registro **no interfiere** con el flujo normal de logout del interceptor ni con el manejo de errores\n\n### Estados finales\n- **TypeScript**: 0 errores\n- **Mobile tests**: 36 passing\n- **Backend tests**: 58 passing

## Resumen\n\nEl problema era que la **pesta├▒a Repartos** (que muestra las entregas del d├¡a) estaba usando el hook `usePedidosDelDia` del feature `pedidos`, el cual llama a `GET /pedidos/hoy`. Eso significa que consum├¡a de la **API de pedidos** cuando deber├¡a consumir de la **API de repartos**.\n\n### Qu├® se cambi├│\n\n**`features/repartos/screens/RepartosListScreen.tsx`**\n\n| Antes | Despu├®s |\n|---|---|\n| `import { usePedidosDelDia } from '@/features/pedidos/hooks/usePedidos'` | `import { useReparto } from '@/features/repartos/hooks/useReparto'` |\n| `const { data: pedidos, ... } = usePedidosDelDia()` | `const { data: reparto, ... } = useReparto(); const pedidos = reparto?.pedidos ?? []` |\n\nAhora el flujo es:\n1. **Repartos tab** ÔåÆ `useReparto` ÔåÆ `GET /repartos` ÔåÆ devuelve un `Reparto` con sus `pedidos[]`\n2. **Pedidos tab** ÔåÆ `useBuscarPedidos` ÔåÆ `GET /pedidos` ÔåÆ devuelve la lista general (esto ya estaba bien)\n\n### Vertex del cambio\n\n- `RepartosListScreen` ya no importa nada del feature `pedidos` ÔÇö ahora depende solo de `repartos/hooks/useReparto`\n- El mock data (`repartoMockData.ts`) ya ten├¡a `pedidos[]` dentro del `Reparto`, as├¡ que no necesit├│ cambios\n- **TypeScript**: 0 errores\n- **Mobile tests**: 36 passing\n- **Backend tests**: 58 passing
